
Results of the calculations presented in the figures and tables of 
"Structure of even-even nuclei using a mapped collective Hamiltonian and the D1S Gogny interaction",
J.-P. Delaroche, M.Girod, J.Libert, H.Goutte, S.Hilaire, S.Péru, N.Pillet, and G.F.Bertsch, 
submitted for publication to Phys.Rev.C (2009), are tabulated below.
The table is also posted on the EPAPS repository, Document No.[??????????].
The quantities tabulated are listed by column.
The figures and tables that make use of the various quantities are also indicated.


	Entries 							Notations			Tables 				Figures
